Refuting Existence and Qualification as the Dependent
Sanusi refutes the second and third divisions of the dependent.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand why neither existence nor the qualification of quiddity by existence can be the thing that depends on an efficient cause, and how these refutations rely on the same logic used against quiddity.

Core Idea
Existence and qualification are not real dependents—they collapse into quiddity or regress.

The author has already refuted the idea that quiddity itself is the dependent. Now he tackles two other possibilities: that existence is dependent, or that the qualification of quiddity by existence is dependent. Both are shown to be impossible through the same arguments already established. This passage tightens the case that nothing in the chain of dependence can escape pointing back to a self-sufficient creator.

Guided Path
1
Read the passage and translation
First read the Arabic source alongside the literal translation to get the flow of the argument. Notice how the author structures the refutation in two main divisions, each with its own reasoning.
Pay attention to the technical terms: الوجود, موصوفية, التسلسل.
2
Identify the three possibilities being refuted
The passage refers back to a previous division. The first possibility (quiddity) was already refuted. Here, the second is existence, and the third is the qualification of quiddity by existence. Identify each and see how the refutations differ.
3
Understand the refutation of the second division
The author argues that existence itself is a quiddity, so the same arguments that refuted quiddity also refute existence. Make sure you see why existence can't be a dependent without leading to regress.
4
Understand the two refutations of the third division
The third division is refuted from two angles: first, the qualification is not a real additional attribute, so it cannot be an effect. Second, even if it were an attribute, it would lead to regress or circularity. Walk through each argument step by step.
5
Reflect on the overall argument
After studying both refutations, consider how they collectively show that every candidate for the dependent (quiddity, existence, qualification) fails. This reinforces the doctrine that only the Necessary Being is independent.
This is a key step in establishing tawhid in the context of causality.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وأما القسم الثاني: وهو أن يقال المحتاج إلى المؤثر والجاعل يمتنع أن يكون هو الوجود. فهذا أيضاً باطل لأن الوجود من حيث إنه وجود: ماهية من الماهيات، وحقيقة من الحقائق، والدليلان المذكوران في امتناع كون الماهية مجعولة يجريان بعينهما في امتناع كون الوجود مجعولاً. وأما القسم الثالث: وهو أن يقال المحتاج إلى الفاعل، والجاعل والمؤثر هو موصوفية الماهية بالوجود فنقول: هذا أيضاً باطل من وجهين: الأول: إن موصوفية الماهية بالوجود ليس أمراً زائداً على الماهية وعلى الوجود، وإذا كان كذلك امتنع الحكم عليها بكونها مجعولة. بيان الأول: إنه لو كانت موصوفية الماهية بالوجود أمراً زائداً مغايراً لهما، لكانت موصوفية الماهية بتلك الموصوفية مغايرة، ولزم التسلسل. وبيان الثاني: إن هذه الموصوفية لما لم تكن أمراً ثبوتياً مغايراً، فإنه يمتنع القول بكونها أثراً للفاعل والجاعل، وذلك باطل، لأن ما لا ثبوت له في نفسه، كيف يعقل جعله أثراً للمؤثر والفاعل؟ الوجه الثاني: في إبطال قوله: الواقع بالفاعل هو موصوفية الماهية بالوجود، أن نقول: هذه الموصوفية إما أن تكون أمراً وجودياً، وإما أن لا تكون، فإن كان أمراً وجودياً فحينئذ يكون له ماهية، ويكون له وجود، وحينئذ يعود التقسيم المذكور فيه من أن الواقع بالفاعل، إما ماهيته أو وجوده، فيكون التسلسل أو الدور.
As for the second division: that it is said the one in need of the effect and agent cannot be existence. This too is false, because existence as existence is a quiddity among quiddities and a reality among realities, and the two proofs mentioned concerning the impossibility of the quiddity being made run identically in the impossibility of existence being made. As for the third division: that it is said the one in need of the agent, maker, and effect is the qualification of quiddity by existence. We say: This too is false from two aspects. The first: The qualification of quiddity by existence is not an additional thing over the quiddity and over existence; and if so, it is impossible to judge it as being made. Clarification of the first: If the qualification of quiddity by existence were an additional thing different from them, then the qualification of quiddity by that qualification would be different, and infinite regress would follow. And clarification of the second: Since this qualification is not a positive (thubuti) thing different, it is impossible to say it is an effect of the agent and maker, and that is false, because whatever has no subsistence in itself, how can it be intelligible to make it an effect of the effect and agent? The second aspect: In refuting his statement: 'What is realized by the agent is the qualification of quiddity by existence,' we say: This qualification either is an existential thing or not. If it is an existential thing, then it has a quiddity and has existence, and then the aforementioned division returns into it: that what is realized by the agent is either its quiddity or its existence, so there would be regress or circularity.
Source pages p. 98

Commentary
This passage continues the refutation of the fifth doubt, now addressing the second and third divisions. The second division claims that existence (wujud) itself is the dependent. The author dismisses this: existence as such is a quiddity and reality, so the same proofs against quiddity apply—existence cannot be 'made' because it is a quiddity. The third division claims that the dependent is the qualification of quiddity by existence (mawsufiyyah). The author gives two refutations. First, this qualification is not a real, additional thing; it is merely a relation. If it were additional, infinite regress would arise. Since it is not a fixed (thubuti) entity, it cannot be an effect. Second, even if one insists it is a real attribute, then it itself would have a quiddity and existence, leading to the same division and hence regress or circularity. Thus all three possibilities are impossible, so the original doubt fails.

Key Terms
الوجود
موصوفية الماهية بالوجود
التسلسل
الدور
الأمر الثبوتي

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: The qualification of quiddity by existence (mawsufiyyah) is a real attribute that can be caused independently.
Correction: The author argues it is not an additional real thing; it is merely a relation or an aspect that has no independent subsistence, so it cannot be an effect.

Checkpoint
What does the first proof of the third division argue about the qualification of quiddity by existence?
A) It is a real attribute that can be made.
B) It is not an additional thing over quiddity and existence.
C) It is identical to existence.
D) It is the same as quiddity.

Key Takeaway
Neither existence nor the qualification of quiddity by existence can be the dependent—they either reduce to quiddity or lead to regress, so only the Necessary Being is truly independent.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
In your daily life, what do you unconsciously rely upon as if it were the ultimate cause of your security or success? How does this lesson's argument that only the Necessary Being is truly independent shake that assumption? Will you actively remind yourself of this when you feel anxious about created means?
?
Consider a time you attributed a result to a secondary cause without acknowledging Allah as the true agent. How does the refutation of 'qualification of quiddity by existence' expose the error of seeing cause and effect as independent? What specific step will you take this week to train your heart to see Allah behind every apparent cause?
?
The lesson shows that even 'existence' itself cannot be the dependent—it is a quiddity. What does this imply about your own existence? Are you living as if your existence is self-sufficient or a gift continuously sustained? If you truly believed you had no independent subsistence, how would your attitude toward Allah's commands change today?

6 min
Refutation of the Third Division: Qualification of Essence by Existence
Sanusi refutes the third division with two aspects: non-addition and existence dilemma.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand why the qualification of the essence by existence cannot be the effect of the agent, according to two distinct arguments.

Core Idea
The qualification is either not an extra thing or leads to regress—either way it cannot be an effect.

The third division proposes that what is in need of an agent is the very qualification of the essence by existence. Sanusi refutes this with two independent arguments: first, this qualification is not an additional positive reality, and second, if it were, it would lead to an infinite regress or reintroduce the original problem. These arguments show that the qualification cannot serve as the effect of the agent.

Guided Path
1
Read the passage carefully
Read the Arabic passage for the third division refutation. Then read the translation. Notice the two main aspects (الوجه الأول and الوجه الثاني).
The passage begins with 'وأما القسم الثالث' and ends just before 'وأما القسم الرابع'.
2
Identify the two aspects of the argument
The first aspect argues that the qualification is not an additional thing; the second poses a dilemma about its existence. Under each, find the sub-arguments.
The first aspect has two explanations: one about infinite regress, the other about lacking positive status.
3
Understand why each aspect disproves the claim
Consider how each argument shows that the qualification cannot be a genuine effect. Ask yourself: what must be true for something to be an effect?
The key is that an effect must be a positive, distinct thing—but the qualification fails this test.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وأما القسم الثالث : وهو أن يقال المحتاج إلى الفاعل ، والجاعل والمؤثر هو موصوفية الماهية بالوجود فنقول : هذا أيضاً باطل من وجهين : الأول : إن موصوفية الماهية بالوجود ليس أمراً زائداً على الماهية وعلى الوجود، وإذا كان كذلك امتنع الحكم عليها بكونها مجعولة . بيان الأول : إنه لو كانت موصوفية الماهية بالوجود أمراً زائداً مغايراً لهما، لكانت موصوفية الماهية بتلك الموصوفية مغايرة، ولزم التسلسل . وبيان الثاني : إن هذه الموصوفية لما لم تكن أمراً ثبوتياً مغايراً ، فإنه يمتنع القول بكونها أثراً للفاعل والجاعل ، وذلك باطل، لأن ما لا ثبوت له في نفسه، كيف يعقل جعله أثراً للمؤثر والفاعل ؟ الوجه الثاني : في إبطال قوله : الواقع بالفاعل هو موصوفية الماهية بالوجود، أن نقول : هذه الموصوفية إما أن تكون أمراً وجودياً ، وإما أن لا تكون ، فإن كان أمراً وجودياً فحينئذ يكون له ماهية، ويكون له وجود، وحينئذ يعود التقسيم المذكور فيه من أن الواقع بالفاعل، إما ماهيته أو وجوده، وإن لم يكن له وجود البتة، استحال القول بأن الواقع بالفاعل والجاعل هو هو، فثبت بما ذكرنا : أنه يمتنع القول بأن تأثير الفاعل في الماهية ممتنع، ويمتنع القول بأن تأثيره في الوجود، ويمتنع القول بأن تأثيره في موصوفية الماهية بالوجود . وأما القسم الرابع وهو بيان أنه لما ظهر بطلان الأقسام كان القول بالتأثير والمؤثر باطلا، فتقريره : أن ذلك الأثر لما كان غنيا في ماهيته عن المؤثر، وكان غنياً في وجوده عن المؤثر، وكان غنياً في اتصاف ماهيته بوجوده عن المؤثر، كانت هذه الماهية الموجودة غنية عن المؤثر والفاعل . لأنه متى حصلت الماهية، وحصل الوجود، وحصلت موصوفية الماهية بالوجود، فقد حصلت الماهية الموجودة بدون هذا المؤثر، وهذا الفاعل . وإذا كان كذلك كانت هذه الماهية الموجودة غنية عن المؤثر. وذلك هو المطلوب
As for the third division: that it is said the thing in need of the agent, the maker, and the effecter is the qualification of the essence by existence. So we say: this too is false from two aspects. The first: that the qualification of the essence by existence is not an additional thing beyond the essence and beyond existence, and if it is so, it is impossible to judge it as being made. Explanation of the first: if the qualification of the essence by existence were an additional thing different from them, then the qualification of the essence by that qualification would be different, and an infinite regress would follow. And explanation of the second: since this qualification is not a positive thing different, it is impossible to say that it is an effect of the agent and maker, and that is false, because something that has no positive existence in itself, how can it be understood to be made an effect of the effecter and agent? The second aspect: in refuting his statement: 'what is brought about by the agent is the qualification of the essence by existence', is that we say: this qualification is either an existent thing or not. If it is an existent thing, then it has an essence and it has existence, and then the mentioned division returns regarding it as to whether what is brought about by the agent is its essence or its existence. And if it has no existence at all, it is impossible to say that what is brought about by the agent and maker is it. So it is established by what we have mentioned: that it is impossible to say that the agent's effect in the essence is impossible, and it is impossible to say that his effect is in existence, and it is impossible to say that his effect is in the qualification of the essence by existence. As for the fourth division: it is an exposition that when the falsity of the divisions became apparent, then the statement of effect and effecter is false. Its exposition: that since that effect was independent in its essence from the effecter, and independent in its existence from the effecter, and independent in the being of its essence qualified by its existence from the effecter, then this existing essence is independent from the effecter and agent. Because whenever the essence occurs, and existence occurs, and the qualification of the essence by existence occurs, then the existing essence has occurred without this effecter and this agent. And if it is so, then this existing essence is independent of the effecter. And that is what was sought.
Source pages p. 98

Commentary
This passage is a structured refutation of two divisions concerning what is in need of an efficient cause (al-fāʿil). The author first addresses the third division: the claim that what is in need is the qualification (mawṣūfiyya) of the essence (al-māhiyya) by existence (al-wujūd). He argues it is false from two aspects. First, this qualification is not an additional thing over and above essence and existence; if it were additional, it would itself require qualification by another qualification, leading to infinite regress (al-tasalsul). If it is not a positive (thubūtī) distinct thing, it cannot be an effect because something with no positive reality cannot be made. Second, the qualification is either existent or non-existent. If existent, it has its own essence and existence, and the same division applies: is the effect its essence or its existence? If non-existent, it cannot be the effect at all. So all three possibilities for the effect (essence, existence, qualification) are refuted. Then the fourth division concludes that since the effect is independent in its essence, existence, and the combination from the effecter, the existing essence can occur without any effecter, thus the claim of dependency is false.

Key Terms
ماهية (essence)
وجود (existence)
موصوفية (qualification)
أثر (effect)
فاعل (agent)
تسلسل (infinite regress)
ثبوتي (positive)

Key Terms from Source Passage

Misconception & Correction
Misconception: People may think that the qualification of essence by existence is a distinct attribute that can be caused by an agent.
Correction: The passage shows that this qualification is either not an additional thing (so cannot be an effect) or, if it were additional, it leads to regress or the same problem recurs.

Checkpoint
According to the passage, why is the qualification of the essence by existence not a valid candidate for being the effect of the agent?
A) Because it is purely mental and has no reality.
B) Because it is either not an extra thing or, if it is, it leads to the same division and regress.
C) Because it is identical to the essence itself.
D) Because existence is eternal and cannot be effected.

Key Takeaway
The qualification of essence by existence cannot be the agent's effect because it is either not a distinct positive reality or, if it is, the same problem recurs.

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
When you consider your own existence, do you ever ponder that it is not a separate 'thing' added to you, but rather that you were nothing and then brought into being by Allah? How does this realization affect your humility before Him?
?
If the qualification of your essence by existence is not an additional reality, then your very being is a direct gift from Allah without any intermediary 'creation' separate from Him. Does this make you feel more dependent on Him? How should this change your daily reliance on Him?
?
Sanusi argues that something with no positive existence cannot be an effect. Your own nonexistence before birth was not a thing that could be acted upon. Yet you are now existent by Allah's will. Does this truth awaken in you a gratitude that acknowledges His absolute power over your being? What will you do today to remind yourself of this?

The Fourth Division: Concluding the Falsity of All Divisions
Sanusi concludes that the effect is independent in essence, existence, and qualification, thus no effecter needed.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will understand how the falsity of all divisions leads to the conclusion that the effect is independent of the agent.

Core Idea
If the effect is independent in essence, existence, and combination, then no agent is needed.

Having refuted the three possible candidates for the effect (essence, existence, qualification), Sanusi now concludes that the existing essence as a whole is independent of any effecter. The fourth division argues that since each component is independent, the composite is also independent, implying that an agent is not required for the existence of the effect.

Guided Path
1
Read the fourth division passage
Read the Arabic passage for the fourth division and its translation. Notice how it summarizes the refutation of the previous divisions.
The passage begins with 'وأما القسم الرابع' and ends with 'وذلك هو المطلوب'.
2
Identify the three independencies
The passage states that the effect is independent in its essence, in its existence, and in the qualification of its essence by existence. Underline each claim.
These three correspond to the three divisions refuted earlier.
3
Grasp the conclusion
Since all parts are independent, the whole existing essence occurs without the agent. Thus the claim of dependency is false.
The conclusion is that the effect is independent of the agent, which is what was to be proved.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
وأما القسم الثالث : وهو أن يقال المحتاج إلى الفاعل ، والجاعل والمؤثر هو موصوفية الماهية بالوجود فنقول : هذا أيضاً باطل من وجهين : الأول : إن موصوفية الماهية بالوجود ليس أمراً زائداً على الماهية وعلى الوجود، وإذا كان كذلك امتنع الحكم عليها بكونها مجعولة . بيان الأول : إنه لو كانت موصوفية الماهية بالوجود أمراً زائداً مغايراً لهما، لكانت موصوفية الماهية بتلك الموصوفية مغايرة، ولزم التسلسل . وبيان الثاني : إن هذه الموصوفية لما لم تكن أمراً ثبوتياً مغايراً ، فإنه يمتنع القول بكونها أثراً للفاعل والجاعل ، وذلك باطل، لأن ما لا ثبوت له في نفسه، كيف يعقل جعله أثراً للمؤثر والفاعل ؟ الوجه الثاني : في إبطال قوله : الواقع بالفاعل هو موصوفية الماهية بالوجود، أن نقول : هذه الموصوفية إما أن تكون أمراً وجودياً ، وإما أن لا تكون ، فإن كان أمراً وجودياً فحينئذ يكون له ماهية، ويكون له وجود، وحينئذ يعود التقسيم المذكور فيه من أن الواقع بالفاعل، إما ماهيته أو وجوده، وإن لم يكن له وجود البتة، استحال القول بأن الواقع بالفاعل والجاعل هو هو، فثبت بما ذكرنا : أنه يمتنع القول بأن تأثير الفاعل في الماهية ممتنع، ويمتنع القول بأن تأثيره في الوجود، ويمتنع القول بأن تأثيره في موصوفية الماهية بالوجود . وأما القسم الرابع وهو بيان أنه لما ظهر بطلان الأقسام كان القول بالتأثير والمؤثر باطلا، فتقريره : أن ذلك الأثر لما كان غنيا في ماهيته عن المؤثر، وكان غنياً في وجوده عن المؤثر، وكان غنياً في اتصاف ماهيته بوجوده عن المؤثر، كانت هذه الماهية الموجودة غنية عن المؤثر والفاعل . لأنه متى حصلت الماهية، وحصل الوجود، وحصلت موصوفية الماهية بالوجود، فقد حصلت الماهية الموجودة بدون هذا المؤثر، وهذا الفاعل . وإذا كان كذلك كانت هذه الماهية الموجودة غنية عن المؤثر. وذلك هو المطلوب
As for the third division: that it is said the thing in need of the agent, the maker, and the effecter is the qualification of the essence by existence. So we say: this too is false from two aspects. The first: that the qualification of the essence by existence is not an additional thing beyond the essence and beyond existence, and if it is so, it is impossible to judge it as being made. Checkpoint
According to the fourth division, in how many respects is the effect independent of the effecter?
A) One: in its essence
B) Two: in essence and existence

How This Lesson Applies — to MY Life?
?
In your daily life, do you instinctively attribute the outcomes you experience to your own actions or to other created beings? Reflect on this passage: if the effect is truly independent in its essence, existence, and qualification, then what does that say about the power you assume lies in means? Confess to yourself a specific instance where you relied on an effect rather than the only real Agent.
?
This passage concludes that no effecter is needed for the existing essence. Yet you constantly act as if your efforts are necessary for results. How can you reconcile this teaching with your practice? Write down one area where you can start mentally disconnecting the effect from its apparent cause, turning your trust solely to God.
